This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

    (door-closed kitchen unknown-west)

  )

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry laundry-room corridor bedroom - location
            east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door pantry kitchen west)

    (door corridor laundry-room north)
    (door-open corridor laundry-room)
    (door corridor bedroom east)
    (door-open corridor bedroom)
    (door bedroom corridor west)
    (door-open bedroom corridor)
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry laundry-room corridor bedroom living-room - location
            east west north south - direction)

    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen laundry-room west)

    (door laundry-room corridor south)
    (door-open laundry-room corridor)
    (door corridor laundry-room north)
    (door-open corridor laundry-room)
    (door corridor bedroom east)
    (door-open corridor bedroom)
    (door bedroom corridor west)
    (door-open bedroom corridor)
    ; living-room is visible from kitchen to north, but there appears to be NO door, so do NOT list door/door-open for kitchen/living-room or vice versa

  )

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

    (door-closed kitchen living-room)

  )

You have already generated df and pf files according to the observations.
This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry laundry-room corridor bedroom living-room - location
            east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen laundry-room west)
    (door-open kitchen laundry-room)
    (door laundry-room kitchen east)
    (door-open laundry-room kitchen)
    (door laundry-room corridor south)
    (door-open laundry-room corridor)
    (door corridor laundry-room north)
    (door-open corridor laundry-room)
    (door corridor bedroom east)
    (door-open corridor bedroom)
    (door bedroom corridor west)
    (door-open bedroom corridor)
    ;; There is no door between kitchen and living-room, remove for soundness
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)
